Other Events.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">On December 24, 2025, Walmart Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) was informed that Chris Nicholas, Executive Vice President, President and Chief Executive Officer, Sam&#8217;s Club U.S., entered into a stock trading plan designed to comply with Rule 10b5-1 under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Plan&#8221;). Rule 10b5-1 trading plans permit individuals who are not in possession of material non-public information to adopt a written pre-arranged plan for transactions in securities under specified conditions and for specified periods of time. Under the terms of the Plan, Mr. Nicholas will have no discretion or control over the timing or effectuation of any transactions in Company securities pursuant to the Plan.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Mr. Nicholas&#8217; Plan provides for sales of Company securities as part of his long-term asset diversification, tax, and financial planning strategy and is in accordance with the Company&#8217;s Insider Trading Policy. Under the terms of the Plan, Mr. Nicholas is scheduled to sell 2,900 shares of the Company&#8217;s common stock on a specified date each month over a period of 12 months beginning in April 2026 and continuing through March 2027 at prevailing market prices. Accordingly, the maximum number of shares to be sold under the Plan is 34,800. </span></div><div style="margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Mr. Nicholas continues to be subject to the Company&#8217;s stock ownership guidelines, under which he is required to hold Company stock equal in value to at least five times his base salary. Upon the conclusion of each sale transaction under the Plan, Mr. Nicholas will continue to satisfy the requirements of the Company&#8217;s stock ownership guidelines.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Any transactions under the Plan will be disclosed publicly through Form 144 and Form 4 filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission to the extent required by law.</span></div><div
